  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_119122ab-6172-4df7-9f29-1bbc6e69efa4'
      });
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer18375121840802446976">The clock is ticking. Alex’s time is running out.<br/><br/>Spring has hit Hazel Cove and with it, the pressure of Alex’s impending fate as Liam’s sacrifice is weighing upon her every thought.   <span id="freeText18375121840802446976" style="display:none">The clock is ticking. Alex’s time is running out.<br /><br />Spring has hit Hazel Cove and with it, the pressure of Alex’s impending fate as Liam’s sacrifice is weighing upon her every thought. There’s so much to do and so little time. How do you stop an ancient pure blooded witch?<br /><br />But Liam isn’t Alex’s only problem. She must focus on what she can fix in the little time she has left. She must confront the past and the horrible betrayal Ethan suffered at the hands of a once trusted ally. Alex will do anything necessary to save Ethan. Even brave a trip to the supernatural capital of the world - New Orleans.<br /><br />Voodoo, Hoodoo, witches and spirits are nothing compared to the evil Alex will face in the backwoods of the Louisiana bayou. Will Alex’s desperation to save her family and friends pull her closer to the darkness?<br /><br />Who can Alex trust? Will James’ connections as a witch hunter help or hurt her? Can she fix her relationship with Peter? Or will the deep seeds of betrayal shatter Alex’s life?<br /><br />Wicked Betrayal is the third book in the New England Witch Chronicles series. The final novel in the series, All Hallows Eve, will be released in 2013. For more information, please visit: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.chelseabellingeri.com">www.chelseabellingeri.com</a></span>

<div class='communityQuestion'>
<div class='questionText'>
<a href="/questions/786562-does-anyone-know-why-this-book-is-priced">Does anyone know why this book is priced so high? I went on to Books a Million to purshase this series and found that while 2 of the books from the series are priced in the typical range for paperbacks, the other is $35 and this one is $89 and they are used books from the Marketplace. I looked on Alibras and found the same prices. I find that rather strange for books that were in publication only a few years ago.</a>
</div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer487086070" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3330500403379592475">Okay. I've never been wrong about who is "meant to be together" (I was right about Edward, Peeta, Daniel & many, many more). But I feel that with this series, I might be wrong. I am 100% Team James. The whole witch with the witch hunter is appealing to me & I love it. I really hope I'm not wrong and they do end up together. Because if not my perfect record will be ruined & I'll probably die of sadness. </span>
  <span id="freeText3330500403379592475" style="display:none">Okay. I've never been wrong about who is "meant to be together" (I was right about Edward, Peeta, Daniel &amp; many, many more). But I feel that with this series, I might be wrong. I am 100% Team James. The whole witch with the witch hunter is appealing to me &amp; I love it. I really hope I'm not wrong and they do end up together. Because if not my perfect record will be ruined &amp; I'll probably die of sadness. </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/471493283?book_show_action=true">Dec 06, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer471493283" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8392364018858136706">I could not put this series down!!! I was literally at the gym when I finished the second one and I sat there on the treadmill buying the 3rd so I could start it while I finished my workout.<br/><br/>By the end of each book you can't help but to have to read the next to find out what is going to happen. I am impatiently awaiting the 4th installment. It took me 2 weeks to weeks to read all 3.<br/><br/>You love the main character's. Alex is Strong and even though she has so much to deal with she still keeps going and</span>
  <span id="freeText8392364018858136706" style="display:none">I could not put this series down!!! I was literally at the gym when I finished the second one and I sat there on the treadmill buying the 3rd so I could start it while I finished my workout.<br /><br />By the end of each book you can't help but to have to read the next to find out what is going to happen. I am impatiently awaiting the 4th installment. It took me 2 weeks to weeks to read all 3.<br /><br />You love the main character's. Alex is Strong and even though she has so much to deal with she still keeps going and fighting doing what she has to to protect her family and friends. Peter, her best friend turned boyfriend, is just the right mix of stability,protectiveness, and is sweet and caring. In a way he grounds her. While James is a bit more dangerous, very protective, and is constantly butting heads with Peter to win Alex's affections. Liam is someone who you want to hate but still for some reason can't. He always helps Alex out but in the end with his own ultimate agenda in place. Both Peter and James team up together in this book to help Alex and it is quite interesting to see how it goes between them. You think one minute they are becoming friends and then the next they are back to being enemies. It keeps you guessing.<br /><br />With each new character introduced into each book you fall more in love with them. Each charater is brought in perfectly and at the right times and just makes everything more complete and entertaining. As the Alex grows and evolutions the plots and rest of the characters do the same. </span>
  <a data-text-id="8392364018858136706" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer18378678493851394628"><strong>Couldn't put it down!</strong><br/><br/>This is the third, in a series of four books. I didn't review the first one, because I didn't know how. I didn't review the second because I was in too much of a hurry to start the third. My reviews would have all been similar anyway. I'm really enjoying this series! I wanted a good, witchy book, and I found it here! No dull moments in these books. They kept me wanting to know what was going to happen next, which made them hard to put down. To me, that's the sign of a good b</span>
  <span id="freeText18378678493851394628" style="display:none"><strong>Couldn't put it down!</strong><br /><br />This is the third, in a series of four books. I didn't review the first one, because I didn't know how. I didn't review the second because I was in too much of a hurry to start the third. My reviews would have all been similar anyway. I'm really enjoying this series! I wanted a good, witchy book, and I found it here! No dull moments in these books. They kept me wanting to know what was going to happen next, which made them hard to put down. To me, that's the sign of a good book. I did learn though, that this author likes a serious cliffhanger. I recommend reading the series, just know that it's a commitment to four books, not just one. But that's a bonus, finding a good series is a great thing. I'm really enjoying these, they're fun. I'm moving on to the fourth one right now. </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('rq4M7PA6eq9HCFb3W1ClL33YDBc84ezhVG/xeHfzlEIoeyhHBGyyl9MwUAgPzLnNtb6XmZTRwcYt2tjMsse7kQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('VUrsM4Q3nSwybqYW+WyimzcJmVPqZdid+nCQgE2XZSbTn8iYcGFVFKZWoOmt8L55/28C3UJV9bqDxbk0iKNK9Q==')})
  }

Bess Southerns, an impoverished widow living in Pendle Forest, is haunted by vis<\/span>\n  <span id=\"freeText6981735190424994779\" style=\"display:none\">Daughters of the Witching Hill brings history to life in a vivid and wrenching account of a family sustained by love as they try to survive the hysteria of a witch-hunt. Bess Southerns, an impoverished widow living in Pendle Forest, is haunted by visions and gains a reputation as a cunning woman. Drawing on the Catholic folk magic of her youth, Bess heals the sick and foretells the future. As she ages, she instructs her granddaughter, Alizon, in her craft, as well as her best friend, who ultimately turns to dark magic. When a peddler suffers a stroke after exchanging harsh words with Alizon, a local magistrate, eager to make his name as a witch finder, plays neighbors and family members against one another until suspicion and paranoia reach frenzied heights. Sharratt interweaves well-researched historical details of the 1612 Pendle witch-hunt with a beautifully imagined story of strong women, family, and betrayal.   <span id="freeText4966908704783787569" style="display:none">Chelsea Luna is the author of the bestselling NEW ENGLAND WITCH CHRONICLES, a young adult paranormal romance series comprising of four novels. The Salem Witch Trials of 1692 were an embarrassing stain on America’s revered past. Innocent people were persecuted at the hands of a few overzealous Puritans, but what if real witches existed during those colonial hunts? What if there are witches in present day New England? That’s what Alexandria Ramsey’s crazy grandmother believes. Grandma Claudia claims Alex descends from a long line of New England witches. \n\nModern day witches in Hazel Cove, Massachusetts? Unlikely, but strange things are occurring in the weeks preceding Alex’s seventeenth birthday. Alex is haunted by bizarre recurring nightmares of a man chasing her through the Hazel Cove Cemetery. On a few occasions, when her emotions have spiraled out of control, inanimate objects have shattered around her. But that’s just a coincidence, right? Alex isn’t so sure, especially after a local girl, who supposedly dabbled in witchcraft, was killed in the nearby forest. \n\nAlex knows something strange is happening. With the arrival of a new boy in town, James Van Curen, who is causing problems between Alex and her best friend, Peter, Alex feels like her entire world is on the verge of chaos. Could Alex really be a witch?
